# Discovery Phase 25FS — Read-Only Runtime Validation Harness Static Evidence Rebuild Gate

## Phase status

Status: **Static evidence rebuild gate for Gemini review**

Phase 25FS performs a documentation-only static evidence rebuild using committed documentation files only.

This phase reads committed markdown documentation under `docs/` and constructs a static evidence table from route-like strings found in those documents. It does not inspect application source files, read source files for route evidence, import application modules, execute dependency inventory, execute route listing, execute runtime discovery, execute the harness, invoke routes, start a local server, query a live database, call admin/public APIs, perform browser automation, make network calls, execute crawler activity, execute extraction activity, execute LLM activity, stage candidates, execute candidate decisions, approve candidates for draft, publish public data, mutate a database, change schema files, change migration files, generate types, change package files, or change lockfiles.

Operational reactivation remains blocked.

## Approved baseline

Phase 25FR was approved, committed, and pushed with:

```text
commit=018717b
full_sha=018717b2d2fe29dd988970e07a8ca3d875aebfc9
subject=Document Phase 25FR static evidence rebuild plan
origin_main=018717b2d2fe29dd988970e07a8ca3d875aebfc9
final_status=## main...origin/main
npm_check_status=passed
gemini_review_status=APPROVED
operational_reactivation_status=blocked
```

Phase 25FR planned this documentation-only rebuild gate and prohibited manifest selection, harness edits, runtime validation, route invocation, live database reads, source inspection, and operational reactivation.

## Phase 25FD harness state

The Phase 25FD harness remains:

```text
harness_file=testing/discovery-read-only-runtime-validation-harness.mjs
static_manifest_entries=0
fetch_call_present=false
runtime_validation=false
route_invocation=false
harness_execution=false
operational_reactivation_status=blocked
```

Phase 25FS does not edit this file.

## Rebuild interpretation

The rebuilt table is documentation only.

```text
table_is_manifest=false
table_is_executable_config=false
table_authorizes_manifest_selection=false
ready_rows_authorize_manifest_edit=false
blocked_rows_authorize_manifest_edit=false
context_only_rows_authorize_manifest_edit=false
manifest_population_allowed=false
runtime_validation_allowed=false
route_invocation_allowed=false
operational_reactivation_status=blocked
```

## Fail-closed summary

Every rebuilt row remains blocked from manifest selection.

Reasons include one or more of:

- Method not proven to be `GET` or `HEAD`.
- Static method/path evidence is incomplete.
- Route identity remains static-documentation-only.
- Authentication boundary is not proven to selection standard.
- Earlier-document evidence remains context-only until a future staleness/supersession review.
- Mutation risk is possible or unknown.
- The current phase is not a manifest selection gate.

```text
manifest_entry_selection_supported=false
manifest_edit_supported=false
manifest_population_supported=false
harness_execution_supported=false
runtime_validation_supported=false
route_invocation_supported=false
operational_reactivation_supported=false
```

## Value safety

Phase 25FS includes only static route-like paths, method labels, source document names, classifications, and counts.

It does not include raw response bodies, request headers, response headers, cookies, tokens, sessions, database URLs, environment values, service credentials, secret-like values, full preserved output dumps, or runtime output.

```text
raw_body_output_included=false
raw_header_output_included=false
credential_output_included=false
environment_values_included=false
secret_like_values_included=false
full_preserved_output_dump_included=false
runtime_output_included=false
```

## Recommended next phase

Phase 25FS recommends proceeding next to:

```text
Phase 25FT — Read-Only Runtime Validation Harness Static Evidence Rebuild Review Gate
```

Phase 25FT should remain documentation-only. It should review the rebuilt static evidence table and decide whether the blocked/context-only result should be preserved or whether a separate manifest selection planning gate is justified later.

Phase 25FT must not:

- Edit the harness.
- Populate the manifest.
- Select final manifest entries.
- Execute the harness.
- Invoke routes.
- Start a local server.
- Query live databases.
- Call admin/public APIs.
- Import application modules.
- Inspect application source files.
- Read application source files for route evidence.
- Execute dependency inventory.
- Execute route listing.
- Add fetch calls.
- Add runtime route discovery.
- Change source behavior.
- Publicly publish data.
- Reactivate operations.

Phase 25FS does not recommend:

- Manifest entry selection retry now.

- Manifest population now.

- Runtime route validation.

- Local server startup.

Operational reactivation remains blocked.

5. Phase 25FB was harness design only.
6. Phase 25FC was implementation planning only.

9. Phase 25FF was manifest population planning only.
10. Phase 25FG was a manifest population gate with zero entries added.
11. Phase 25FH was manifest entry selection planning only.
12. Phase 25FI selected zero entries.
13. Phase 25FJ reviewed and accepted the zero-entry result.
14. Phase 25FK planned the static evidence table structure.
15. Phase 25FL constructed a documentation-only zero-row static evidence table.
16. Phase 25FM reviewed that zero-row table as safe but insufficient.
17. Phase 25FN planned source coverage review.
18. Phase 25FO reviewed source coverage and recommended expansion planning only.
19. Phase 25FP planned source expansion decision controls.
20. Phase 25FQ made a documentation-only source-group decision.
21. Phase 25FR planned the static evidence rebuild.
22. Phase 25FS rebuilt the static evidence table documentation-only.
23. Runtime validation harness execution has not occurred.
24. Runtime route validation has not occurred.
25. Live database validation has not started.
26. Candidate pipeline execution has not started.
27. Public publishing has not started.
28. No reactivation gate has been approved.

Gemini decision: APPROVED.

Gemini confirmed that Phase 25FS:

- Preserves the approved Phase 25EV through Phase 25FR chain.
- Remains strictly documentation-only.
- Uses only committed documentation files.
- Keeps the Phase 25FD harness inert and empty-manifest.
- Successfully rebuilds the static evidence table from committed documentation.
- Avoids all excluded runtime, source, API, database, browser, and network operations.
- Keeps all 470 rebuilt rows blocked from manifest selection.
- Preserves the fail-closed posture.
- Correctly identifies Phase 25FT as the next documentation-only static evidence rebuild review gate.
- Keeps operational reactivation blocked.
- Correctly handled the false-positive scanner recovery by using a stricter key detector after the filename `risk-review-planning-gate.md` triggered the overly broad `sk-` pattern.
